            var _obj = obj || this,

            if (_keyChain.length &gt; 1){
                _parentKey = _keyChain.shift();
                _parentObj = _obj[_parentKey];

                    }
                    else if (_value === "false") {
                        _valueLowerCase = false;
                        _value = _valueLowerCase;
                    }
                }
            }

            return _value;
        };

<!-- custom JS -->
<script>

  requirejs.config( {
    "paths": {
      "tween": "https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/gsap/1.19.1/TweenMax.min"
    },
    "shim": {
      "tween": {
        "deps": ["jquery"], "exports": "TweenMax"
      }
    }
  });

  require(['tween'], function() {

    $(document).ready(function(){

      var $obj = $(".modal"),
          $dObj = $("#dynamicModal"),
          $overlay = $(".modal-overlay");

      function getPos() {
        return $obj.position();
      }

      var lastPos = getPos();

      function update() {
        var pos = getPos();
        var limit = 20;
        var dx = Math.min(limit, Math.abs(pos.left - lastPos.left) * 0.5);
        var dy = Math.min(limit, Math.abs(pos.top - lastPos.top) * 0.5);
        // setBlur(dx+","+dy);

        lastPos = pos;
        requestAnimationFrame(update);
      }

      update();

      var isOpen = false;

      function openModal() {
        /*$overlay.css({
          display:"block"
        })*/
        TweenMax.to($overlay, 0.1, {autoAlpha: 1});

        TweenMax.fromTo($obj, .75, {y: -($(document).height() + $dObj.height())}, {
          delay: 0.15,
          y: "0%",
          ease: Power2.easeIn
        });
      }

      function closeModal() {
        TweenMax.to($overlay, 0.1, {delay: 0.55, autoAlpha: 0});
        TweenMax.to($obj, 0.55, {y: -($(document).height() + $dObj.height()), ease: Back.easeIn});
      }

      $(".open-modal").click(function () {
        openModal();
      })
      $(".close-modal,.modal-overlay").click(function () {
        closeModal();
      })


      function sendMyAjax(URL_address){

        $('body').on('click touchstart', '.promo-detail-btn', function(e){
          // AJAX calls to dynamic url
          var URL_address = $(this).attr('data-page') + '.html';
          var jaxed = $(this).attr('data-loaded-content');
          var dynamicClass = $(this).attr('data-loaded-class');

          openModal();
          $('.modal').css('min-height', '245px');
          $.ajax({
            url: URL_address,
            dataType: 'html',
            cache: false, // cache to false helps function on mobile
            beforeSend: function(){
            },
            success: function(data){
              var div =  $(data).find(jaxed);
              $('.dynamic-content').html(div);
              $('#loadPromo').css('visibility', 'hidden');
            }
          });
        });
      }; // end AJAX function

      $('.promo-detail-btn').click(sendMyAjax); // load content via AJAX function

    });
  });// end require call for tween

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
		requirejs.config( {
  "paths": {
    "TweenMax": "https://www.vans.com/ns/vans/js/TweenMax"
  },
  "shim": {
    "TweenMax": {
      "deps": ["jquery"], "exports": "TweenMax"
    }
  }
});

require(["TweenMax"], function() {
  $(document).ready(function() {

    /**
     * touch/mobile detection
     * adds class to html if/if not touch
     */
    var touchsupport = ('ontouchstart' in window) || (navigator.maxTouchPoints &gt; 0) || (navigator.msMaxTouchPoints &gt; 0)
    if (!touchsupport) { // browser doesn't support touch
      document.documentElement.className += " nontouch"
    } else {
      document.documentElement.className += " touch"
    }

    /**
     * IE detection
     */
      // Get IE or Edge browser version
    var version = detectIE();

    if (version === false) {
      document.documentElement.className += " not-ie";
    }
    /**
     * detect IE
     * returns version of IE or false, if browser is not Internet Explorer
     */
    function detectIE() {
      var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;

      var msie = ua.indexOf('MSIE ');
      if (msie &gt; 0) {
        // IE 10 or older =&gt; return version number
        return parseInt(ua.substring(msie + 5, ua.indexOf('.', msie)), 10);
      }

      var trident = ua.indexOf('Trident/');
      if (trident &gt; 0) {
        // IE 11 =&gt; return version number
        var rv = ua.indexOf('rv:');
        return parseInt(ua.substring(rv + 3, ua.indexOf('.', rv)), 10);
      }

      var edge = ua.indexOf('Edge/');
      if (edge &gt; 0) {
        // Edge (IE 12+) =&gt; return version number
        return parseInt(ua.substring(edge + 5, ua.indexOf('.', edge)), 10);
      }

      // other browser
      return false;
    }

// add class to mobile overlay content
$('.overlay-content.below-image').addClass('overlay-header');

// add class to secondary button
if ( ($('.overlay-content h3').length &gt; 0) &amp;&amp; ($('.overlay-content h6').length &gt; 0)  ){
  $('.overlay-content a.secondary.button').addClass('wht');
}

// wrap header text multiline background image
$('.row.overlay-content h6').wrapInner('&lt;span&gt;');
// make content copy block visible
$('.row.overlay-content &gt; div').css('opacity', 1);

function notMobile() {
    if (window.matchMedia('(min-width: 768px)').matches) {

      equalheight = function(container) {

        var currentTallest = 0,
          currentRowStart = 0,
          rowDivs = new Array(),
          $el,
          topPosition = 0;
        $(container).each(function() {

          $el = $(this);
          $($el).height('auto')
          topPostion = $el.position().top;

          if (currentRowStart != topPostion) {
            for (currentDiv = 0; currentDiv &lt; rowDivs.length; currentDiv++) {
              rowDivs[currentDiv].height(currentTallest);
            }
            rowDivs.length = 0; // empty the array
            currentRowStart = topPostion;
            currentTallest = $el.height();
            rowDivs.push($el);
          } else {
            rowDivs.push($el);
            currentTallest = (currentTallest &lt; $el.height()) ? ($el.height()) : (currentTallest);
          }
          for (currentDiv = 0; currentDiv &lt; rowDivs.length; currentDiv++) {
            rowDivs[currentDiv].height(currentTallest);
          }
        });
      }

      $(window).on('load', function() {
        equalheight('.espot__text');
        equalheight('.shop-section__col--outer');
      });


      $(window).on('resize', function() {
        equalheight('.espot__text');
        equalheight('.shop-section__col--outer');
      });

    }
  }

  /* Call the function */
  notMobile();
  /* Attach the function to the resize event listener */
  window.addEventListener('resize', notMobile, false);

if(window.matchMedia('(max-width: 640px)').matches) {
    /**
     * accordion nav
     */
    // activate accordion for shop links on mobile
    $('.shop-section__col').each( function() {

      var acc_btn = $(this).find('.shop-section__title');
      var acc = $(this).find('.shop-section__links');

      $(acc_btn).click(function(){
        acc.slideToggle();
        $(this).toggleClass('expanded');
        $(this).closest('.shop-section__col--outer').toggleClass('expanded');
      });
    });
  }

  }); // end doc ready
}); // end require call
